 // 2^n_bits\n    registers_.assign(num_registers_, 0);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes binary.\n *\n * @param[in] hash\n * @returns binary of a given hash\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {\n  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes leading zeros.\n *\n * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset\n * @returns leading zeros of given binary set\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Find the position of the leftmost 1 bit (counting from the right, starting at 1)\n  // This is equivalent to: leading_zeros(bset) + 1\n  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; The first 1 bit in 0x20000 sits at position 17 from the right, meaning 46 leading zeros in the full 64-bit representation. Applying the formula gives lz_in_actual_bits = 46 - 1.\n\nThe test expects dense_bucket[0] = 2 and overflow_bucket[0] = 1, but neither interpretation of 46 (splitting as low/high nibbles or using bit shifts) produces these values. This suggests my approach to computing leading zeros might be fundamentally wrong. I should reconsider whether PositionOfLeftmostOne or __builtin_clzll is the right function to use here, or if AddElem even needs ComputeBinary at all.\n\nLet me try stripping out the unused ComputeBinary and PositionOfLeftmostOne methods and using built-in functions directly instead. **Redundant state**: state that duplicates existing state, cached values that could be derived, observers/effects that could be direct calls\n2. **Parameter sprawl**: adding new parameters to a function instead of generalizing or restructuring existing ones\n3. **Copy-paste with slight variation**: near-duplicate code blocks that should be unified with a shared abstraction\n4. **Leaky abstractions**: exposing internal details that should be encapsulated, or breaking existing abstraction boundaries\n5. **Stringly-typed code**: using raw strings where constants, enums (string unions), or branded types already exist in the codebase\n\n### Agent 3: Efficiency Review\n\nReview the same changes for efficiency:\n\n1. **Unnecessary work**: redundant computations, repeated file reads, duplicate network/API calls, N+1 patterns\n2. **Missed concurrency**: independent operations run sequentially when they could run in parallel\n3. **Hot-path bloat**: new blocking work added to startup or per-request/per-render hot paths\n4. **Unnecessary existence checks**: pre-checking file/resource existence before operating (TOCTOU anti-pattern) — operate directly and handle the error\n5. **Memory**: unbounded data structures, missing cleanup, event listener leaks\n6. **Overly broad operations**: reading entire files when only a portion is needed, loading all items when filtering for one\n\n## Phase 3: Fix Issues\n\nWait for all three agents to complete.  // 2^n_bits\n    dense_bucket_.assign(num_registers_, 0);\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Element is added for HLL calculation. */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract the register index from the first n_bits bits\n  uint32_t register_idx = hash & ((1U << n_bits_) - 1);  // Lower n_bits bits\n\n  // Get the remaining bits (shift out the first n_bits)\n  hash_t remaining_bits = hash >> n_bits_;\n\n  // Find the position of the first 1 bit (counting from 1 on the right)\n  // This is equivalent to: 64 - leading_zeros\n  uint64_t rho;\n  if (remaining_bits == 0) {\n    rho = 64 - n_bits_;  // All remaining bits are zero\n  } else {\n    // Count leading zeros using __builtin_clzll and compute position\n    rho = 64 - __builtin_clzll(remaining_bits);\n  }\n\n  // Presto encoding: split the rho value into dense (4-bit) and overflow (3-bit) parts\n  // Dense bucket stores the lower 4 bits (0-15)\n  // Overflow bucket stores the upper bits (0-7)\n  uint8_t dense_value = rho & 0x0F; i < num_registers_; ++i) {\n    // Reconstruct the rho value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_value = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_value = 0;\n\n    auto it = overflow_bucket_.find(i);\n    if (it != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_value = it->second.to_ullong();\n    }\n\n    // Reconstruct: rho = (overflow_value << 4) | dense_value\n    uint64_t rho = (overflow_value << 4) | dense_value;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality estimation: α * m² / sum\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_registers_);\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(CONSTANT * m * m / sum);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":65,"oldLines":13,"newStart":65,"newLines":9,"lines":["   }"," ","   // Update overflow bucket","-  std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE> current_overflow(0);","-  if (overflow_bucket_.count(register_idx) > 0) {","-    current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[register_idx];","-  }","   std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE> new_overflow(overflow_value);","-","-  if (new_overflow.to_ullong() > current_overflow.to_ullong()) {","+  auto it = overflow_bucket_.find(register_idx);","+  if (it == overflow_bucket_.end() || new_overflow.to_ullong() > it->second.to_ullong()) {","     overflow_bucket_[register_idx] = new_overflow;","   }"," }"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

i < num_registers_; ++i) {\n    // Reconstruct the rho value from dense and overflow buckets\n    uint64_t dense_value = dense_bucket_[i].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_value = 0;\n\n    auto it = overflow_bucket_.find(i);\n    if (it != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_value = it->second.to_ullong();\n    }\n\n    // Reconstruct: rho = (overflow_value << 4) | dense_value\n    uint64_t rho = (overflow_value << 4) | dense_value;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(rho));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality estimation: α * m² / sum\n  double m = static_cast<double>(num_registers_);\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(CONSTANT * m * m / sum);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":75,"oldLines":7,"newStart":75,"newLines":7,"lines":[" /** @brief Function to compute cardinality. */"," template <typename T>"," auto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {","-  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {","+  if (n_bits_ < 0) {","     cardinality_ = 0;","     return;","   }"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}
